		}
		complete_effect = {
			SZC = {
				every_core_state = {
					remove_core_of = SZC
				}
			}
			release = SZC
			601 = { add_core_of = SZC }
			605 = { add_core_of = SZC }
			650 = { add_core_of = SZC }
			661 = { add_core_of = SZC }
			788 = { add_core_of = SZC }
			1049 = { add_core_of = SZC }

			SZC = { 
				every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
					NOT = { 
						is_core_of = SIC
					}
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = SIC
						OWNER = { is_subject_of = SIC} 
					}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = SZC
				}
			}
			SZC = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = SZC_ROME_OCC
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

				set_popularities = {
					syndicalist = 0

					}
				}

				save_global_event_target_as = Asia_Proconsularis

				}
			}
